  // Immediate self-invoking function to attempt an early removal
  (function() {
   var styleTag = document.getElementById('kl-custom-fonts');
   if (styleTag) {
    styleTag.remove();
   }
  })();

  // Using MutationObserver for dynamic tags
  (function() {
   var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
    mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
     if (mutation.addedNodes) {
      mutation.addedNodes.forEach(function(node) {
       if (node.id === 'kl-custom-fonts' && node.tagName === 'STYLE') {
        node.remove();
        observer.disconnect(); // Disconnect the observer when found and removed
       }
      });
     }
    });
   });

   observer.observe(document, { childList: true, subtree: true });

See More Testimonials    Property Management Software FAQs  What is property management software?Property management software is a free or paid-by-the-unit solution that enables landlords and property managers to market properties, screen tenants, collect rent, and much more from a single location.    These cloud-based systems offer a centralized location to complete management tasks. With TurboTenant, landlords can market their properties to dozens of sites with a single click, field rental applicants from around the U.S., show their property, screen those they’re most interested in, create and sign a lease agreement, collect rent, and track all their finances — in one place.    And with mobile apps, landlords and tenants can find all their most important details, including their lease agreement, from anywhere. The result is far less time spent digging through emails, sorting through text messages, and wondering where that document went. Plus, communication happens in the same place, so you and your tenants are always on the same page.    Ultimately, the best property management software helps small landlords, big landlords, and everyone in between by streamlining their processes to make running their residential property management businesses more efficient. And with TurboTenant’s free option, there’s no risk in trying it.    Don’t believe us? Check out our glowing reviews on Reviews.io and see why 90% of people who use TurboTenant recommend it to others. Or, sign up for a free account today and take it for a spin. You don’t need a credit card and can start listing properties immediately.    What are the benefits of using property management software?For time-strapped landlords and property managers of all stripes, the key benefit of using all-in-one software for property management solution boils down to time savings. You’ll be much more efficient at running your business because you can automate the mundane everyday tasks that eat your time.  Let’s break down a few more benefits you’ll gain from property manager software.  Tenant Management  Using the best rental property management software, like TurboTenant, provides tenants with a portal from which they can submit maintenance requests, pay rent, and review their lease. It empowers tenants and helps them feel heard when issues arise.  Financial Management  A spreadsheet can be helpful; there’s no doubt about it. But, when you can link all of the financial aspects of your property management business into a single location, you won’t need to input figures manually.  Instead, when rent payments flow in, they’re automatically tracked as revenue, and when you have an expense, the property management software accounts for it. It’s an easy way to improve your financial accuracy so you always know where you stand.  Scalability  It’ll be challenging if you intend to grow from a small landlord to a big one unless you use software. As the number of properties you own grows, the administrative work to manage them does as well.  Property management software reduces your workload. As your number of properties increases, the software’s automation handles all the tedious manual work that would require you to hire help or spend your long nights doing it yourself.  Improved Tenant Satisfaction  Most tenants are used to paying for things online; why should rent be any different? Providing them with the tools to pay their rent via ACH, debit, or credit card modernizes your business over checks and money orders and gives your tenants options.  According to internal TurboTenant data, 66.09% of tenants pay their rent via debit card, ACH, or credit card. It’s essential to provide tenants with the tools they need to complete their most critical task: paying rent, and TurboTenant’s free property management software can help you do that.    What features should I look for in property management software?For most landlords and property managers, six key property management software features will help you control the chaos of running your residential properties and help you gain more time back for the things you want to do. They are:  Property Marketing  TurboTenant’s property management software can take a single listing and distribute it to dozens of listing sites with a single click. For you, that means you won’t need to create and disperse listings individually.  Rental Applications  With online rental applications, you can simply send prospective tenants a link to apply to your property — no more stopping at the print shop to pick up applications.  Tenant Screening  Investment properties are more than just housing. They’re your retirement, nest egg, or wealth-generation vehicle. Don’t trust renting them to just anybody. TurboTenant’s online property management software enables you to screen tenants quickly so you can fully understand their credit health, criminal history, and eviction record (where allowed by law) and feel confident about who’s renting your place.  Lease Agreements  A non-compliant lease agreement can spell trouble for landlords. TurboTenant offers lawyer-approved leases that help you set the rights and responsibilities for you and your tenant from the jump.    Plus, you can e-sign it from anywhere, speeding up the process of locking in your next great tenant. From the landlord portal within our property managing software platform, you can manage each lease for every tenant so you always know their statuses.  Online Rent Collection  Collecting rent can be a hassle. And the more tenants you have, the more trouble it becomes. With TurboTenant’s online rent collection feature, your tenants can pay their rent online and even set up autopay, automating the process of collecting rent.    Plus, our rent collection software lets you send automatic rent reminders, apply late fees, and distribute receipts digitally. It might be the most important property management software feature of them all.  Accounting  TurboTenant accounting enables you to get rid of those spreadsheets and Quickbooks and, finally, utilize tools built specifically for property managers and landlords. With it, you can automate the most tedious aspects of running your business.    Then, with just a few clicks, generate reports that make tax time less stressful.    Who is property management software built for?TurboTenant built its residential management software for anybody who manages a property. You could be a small business owner or landlord with a property or two and find value in its automations. Or you could be a property management company with a portfolio of properties and lean on TurboTenant’s robust tenant and lease tracking features to help you stay ahead of the game.    It depends on your unique needs, but if you manage property, TurboTenant is for you.  How does TurboTenant offer its software for free?  TurboTenant’s free online property management software is offered to landlords for free because we collect fees from tenants. TurboTenant makes money by collecting and keeping the screening fee that tenants pay when they apply to properties. Because we buy screening reports in bulk at a cheaper rate than landlords, we make a small profit from each one.    Further, TurboTenant makes money on each rent payment submitted in its free tier. Our Premium tier waives ACH fees.    Property management software is a free or paid-by-the-unit solution that enables landlords and property managers to market properties, screen tenants, collect rent, and much more from a single location.    These cloud-based systems offer a centralized location to complete management tasks. With TurboTenant, landlords can market their properties to dozens of sites with a single click, field rental applicants from around the U.S., show their property, screen those they’re most interested in, create and sign a lease agreement, collect rent, and track all their finances — in one place.    And with mobile apps, landlords and tenants can find all their most important details, including their lease agreement, from anywhere. The result is far less time spent digging through emails, sorting through text messages, and wondering where that document went. Plus, communication happens in the same place, so you and your tenants are always on the same page.  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(event) {  
 const setTrackingCookie = (name, value, days) => {
  const expires = new Date();
  expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000); // Set to expire in 8 hours
  document.cookie = name + '=' + value + ';expires=' + expires.toUTCString() + ';path=/;domain=.turbotenant.com';
 };

 const getUrlParameter = (name) => {
  name = name.replace(/[\[]/, '\\[').replace(/[\]]/, '\\]');
  const regex = new RegExp('[\\?&]' + name + '=([^&#]*)');
  const results = regex.exec(location.search);
  return results === null ? '' : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
 }
 
 const getDeviceDetails = () => {
  const userAgent = navigator.userAgent;
  const deviceType = /iPad|iPhone|iPod/.test(userAgent) && !window.MSStream ? 'iOS Device' : /android/i.test(userAgent) ? 'Android Device' : 'Desktop';
 
  let operatingSystem = "Unknown OS";
  if (userAgent.indexOf("Win") != -1) operatingSystem = "Windows";
  if (userAgent.indexOf("Mac") != -1) operatingSystem = "MacOS";
  if (userAgent.indexOf("X11") != -1) operatingSystem = "UNIX";
  if (userAgent.indexOf("Linux") != -1) operatingSystem = "Linux";
 
  return { deviceType, operatingSystem };
 }
 
 const getClickID = () => {
  const gclid = getUrlParameter('gclid');
  const msclkid = getUrlParameter('msclkid');
  const fbclid = getUrlParameter('fbclid');
  const impact = getUrlParameter('irclickid');
  const shareSale = getUrlParameter('sscid');
 
  if (gclid) return { type: 'Gclid', value: gclid };
  if (msclkid) return { type: 'Msclkid', value: msclkid };
  if (fbclid) return { type: 'FBclid', value: fbclid };
  if (impact) return { type: 'Impact', value: impact };
  if (shareSale) return { type: 'ShareSale', value: shareSale };

  return null;
 }

 const landingPage = window.location.href;
 const pathName = window.location.pathname;
 const referrerUrl = window.document.referrer;
 const source = getUrlParameter('utm_source') || null;
 const medium = getUrlParameter('utm_medium') || null;
 const campaign = getUrlParameter('utm_campaign') || null;
 const term = getUrlParameter('utm_term') || null;
 const content = getUrlParameter('utm_content') || null;
 const clickID = getClickID();
 const { deviceType, operatingSystem } = getDeviceDetails();
 
 const collectedData = {
  landingPage,
  pathName,
  source,
  medium,
  campaign,
  term,
  content,
  clickID,
  deviceType,
  operatingSystem,
  referrerUrl
 };

 const trackingCookieName = 'signup_tracking';

 const storedSessionValue = sessionStorage.getItem('ttsession');

 if (!storedSessionValue) {
  sessionStorage.setItem('ttsession', '1');
  setTrackingCookie(trackingCookieName, JSON.stringify(collectedData));
 }       
});

   function videoSEOGenerateYouTubeThumbnail( id ) {
    var thumbnail = '<picture class="video-seo-youtube-picture">\n' +
     '<source class="video-seo-source-to-maybe-replace" media="(min-width: 801px)" srcset="https://i.ytimg.com/vi/' + id + '/maxresdefault.jpg" >\n' +
     '<source class="video-seo-source-hq" media="(max-width: 800px)" srcset="https://i.ytimg.com/vi/' + id + '/hqdefault.jpg">\n' +
     '<img fetchpriority="high" onload="videoSEOMaybeReplaceMaxResSourceWithHqSource( event );" src="https://i.ytimg.com/vi/' + id + '/hqdefault.jpg" width="480" height="360" loading="eager" alt="">\n' +
     '</picture>\n',
     play = '<div class="video-seo-youtube-player-play"></div>';
    return thumbnail.replace( "ID", id ) + play;
   }

   function videoSEOMaybeReplaceMaxResSourceWithHqSource( event ) {
    var sourceMaxRes,
     sourceHighQuality,
     loadedThumbnail = event.target,
     parent = loadedThumbnail.parentNode;

    if ( loadedThumbnail.naturalWidth < 150 ) {
     sourceMaxRes = parent.querySelector(".video-seo-source-to-maybe-replace");
     sourceHighQuality = parent.querySelector(".video-seo-source-hq");
     sourceMaxRes.srcset = sourceHighQuality.srcset;
     parent.className = "video-seo-youtube-picture video-seo-youtube-picture-replaced-srcset";
    }
   }

   function videoSEOYouTubeThumbnailHandleKeydown( event ) {
    if ( event.keyCode !== 13 && event.keyCode !== 32 ) {
     return;
    }

    if ( event.keyCode === 13 ) {
     videoSEOGenerateYouTubeIframe( event );
    }

    if ( event.keyCode === 32 ) {
     event.preventDefault();
    }
   }

   function videoSEOYouTubeThumbnailHandleKeyup( event ) {
    if ( event.keyCode !== 32 ) {
     return;
    }

    videoSEOGenerateYouTubeIframe( event );
   }

   function videoSEOGenerateYouTubeIframe( event ) {
    var el = ( event.type === "click" ) ? this : event.target,
     iframe = document.createElement( "iframe" );

    iframe.setAttribute( "src", "https://www.youtube.com/embed/" + el.dataset.id + "?autoplay=1&enablejsapi=1&origin=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.turbotenant.com" );
    iframe.setAttribute( "frameborder", "0" );
    iframe.setAttribute( "allowfullscreen", "1" );
    iframe.setAttribute( "allow", "accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" );
    el.parentNode.replaceChild( iframe, el );
   }

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
  if (document.body.classList.contains("single-post")) {
    
    const initializeCarousels = () => {
      document.querySelectorAll(".elementor-swiper").forEach(function (el) {
        if (el.swiper) {
          // Destruir y reinicializar en mobile si es necesario
          if (window.innerWidth <= 768) {
            el.swiper.destroy(true, true);
            // Reinicializar después de un breve delay
            setTimeout(() => {
              if (typeof Swiper !== "undefined") {
                // Recrear el swiper con configuración mobile-friendly
                new Swiper(el, {
                  slidesPerView: 'auto',
                  spaceBetween: 10,
                  freeMode: true,
                  // Otras configuraciones según necesites
                });
              }
            }, 100);
          } else {
            el.swiper.update();
          }
        }
      });
    };

    // Ejecutar después de que todo cargue
    setTimeout(initializeCarousels, 1000);
    
    // Re-ejecutar en resize (cambio de orientación)
    window.addEventListener('resize', debounce(initializeCarousels, 300));
  }
});

// Función debounce para evitar múltiples ejecuciones
function debounce(func, wait) {
  let timeout;
  return function executedFunction(...args) {
    const later = () => {
      clearTimeout(timeout);
      func(...args);
    };
    clearTimeout(timeout);
    timeout = setTimeout(later, wait);
  };
}

  const bodyTag = document.body;
        const pageHeader = document.querySelector(".mobile-mega-menu");
        const toggleMenu = pageHeader.querySelector(".toggle-menu");
        const closeMenu = pageHeader.querySelector(".close-menu");
        const menuWrapper = pageHeader.querySelector(".menu-wrapper");
        const level1Links = pageHeader.querySelectorAll(".level-1 > li > a");
        const listWrapper2 = pageHeader.querySelector(".list-wrapper:nth-child(2)");
        const subMenuWrapper2 = listWrapper2.querySelector(".sub-menu-wrapper");
        const backOneLevelBtns = pageHeader.querySelectorAll(".back-one-level");
        const isVisibleClass = "is-visible";
        const isActiveClass = "is-active";
  
  [ toggleMenu, closeMenu ].forEach(function(element) {
      element.addEventListener("click", function() {
   menuWrapper.classList.toggle(isVisibleClass);
   bodyTag.classList.toggle("mobile-mega-active");
   if (!this.classList.contains(isVisibleClass)) {    
    listWrapper2.classList.remove(isVisibleClass);
    const menuLinks = menuWrapper.querySelectorAll("a");
    for (const menuLink of menuLinks) {
    menuLink.classList.remove(isActiveClass);    
    }
   }
     });
  });  


        for (const level1Link of level1Links) {
        level1Link.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
            const siblingList = level1Link.nextElementSibling;
            if (siblingList) {
            e.preventDefault();
            //set the label text
            const text = e.target.textContent.trim();
            document.getElementById("section-label").textContent = text;
            this.classList.add(isActiveClass);
            const cloneSiblingList = siblingList.cloneNode(true);
            subMenuWrapper2.innerHTML = "";
            subMenuWrapper2.append(cloneSiblingList);
            listWrapper2.classList.add(isVisibleClass);
            }
        });
        }

        for (const backOneLevelBtn of backOneLevelBtns) {
        backOneLevelBtn.addEventListener("click", function () {
            const parent = this.closest(".list-wrapper");
            parent.classList.remove(isVisibleClass);
            parent.previousElementSibling
            .querySelector(".is-active")
            .classList.remove(isActiveClass);
        });
        }

style="border-radius: 8px;"> <source src="https://www.turbotenant.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/02/home-esa-loop-cropped.mp4" type="video/mp4" /> </video> </div> <script>
  document.addEventListener(
 "DOMContentLoaded",
 function () {
  var modal        = document.getElementById( 'video_modal_699b0c2c45a51' );
  var modalOverlay = modal.querySelector( '.modal-overlay' );
  var iframe       = document.getElementById( 'video_modal_699b0c2c45a51_iframe' );
  var thumbnail    = document.getElementById( 'video_modal_699b0c2c45a51_thumbnail' );
  var closeButton  = modal.querySelector( '.close' );
  var videoSrc     = iframe.getAttribute( 'data-src' ); // Store the original src for later use

  // Open modal and lazy-load video on button click
  document.getElementById( 'video_modal_699b0c2c45a51_trigger' ).addEventListener(
   'click',
   function () {
    modal.style.display = 'block';
    setTimeout(
     function () {
      modal.style.opacity = 1; },
     10
    ); // Fade in
    document.body.classList.add( 'no-scroll' ); // Disable background scroll

    // Lazy load the iframe video when modal opens
    iframe.setAttribute( 'src', videoSrc ); // Set src again every time modal opens
    iframe.style.display    = 'block';
    thumbnail.style.display = 'none'; // Hide thumbnail once the video loads
   }
  );

  // Close modal and reset video when clicking the close button
  closeButton.addEventListener(
   'click',
   function () {
    youtubeCloseModal();
   }
  );

  // Close modal and reset video when clicking the overlay
  if (modalOverlay) {
   modalOverlay.addEventListener(
    'click',
    function () {
     youtubeCloseModal();
    }
   );
  } else {
   console.error( 'Modal overlay not found.' );
  }

  // Function to close the modal and reset video
  function youtubeCloseModal() {
   modal.style.opacity = 0; // Fade out
   setTimeout(
    function () {
     modal.style.display = 'none';
     document.body.classList.remove( 'no-scroll' ); // Re-enable background scroll

     // Stop the video when closing by clearing the iframe src
     if (iframe) {
      iframe.style.display = 'none'; // Hide iframe while resetting
      iframe.setAttribute( 'src', '' ); // Clear the src to stop the video
      thumbnail.style.display = 'block'; // Show the thumbnail again
     }
    },
    300
   ); // Wait for the fade-out transition
  }
 }
); </script> </div><div class="media_type_mobile"> <div class="video-holder" style="position: relative;border-radius: 8px;"> <div class="dc-hero-wrapper" style="position: absolute;z-index: 1;width:  function initCarousell() {
        // Usamos un intervalo para esperar a que 'carouselInlineWidget' esté definido
        const checkWidgetInterval = setInterval(function() {
            console.log('white visible?', jQuery('.tt-template-white-only').is(':visible'))
            if (typeof carouselInlineWidget !== 'undefined' && typeof jQuery !== 'undefined') {
                clearInterval(checkWidgetInterval);
                
                jQuery(document).ready(function() {
                    const targetId = jQuery('.tt-template-white-only').is(':visible') 
                        ? 'reviewsio-carousel-widget-white' 
                        : 'reviewsio-carousel-widget-dark';
                    
                    console.log('Iniciando widget en target:', targetId);
                    new carouselInlineWidget(targetId, carouselSettings);
                });
            }
        }, 500); // Intenta cada medio segundo
    }
    initCarousell();

With TurboTenant, landlords can market their properties to dozens of sites with a single click, field rental applicants from around the U.S., show their property, screen those they’re most interested in, create and sign a lease agreement, collect rent, and track all their finances — in one place.</p><p>And with mobile apps, landlords and tenants can find all their most important details, including their lease agreement, from anywhere. The result is far less time spent digging through emails, sorting through text messages, and wondering where that document went. Plus, communication happens in the same place, so you and your tenants are always on the same page.</p><p>Ultimately, the best property management software helps landlords streamline their processes to make running their residential property management businesses more efficient. And with TurboTenant’s free option, there’s no risk in trying it.</p><p>Don’t believe us? You don’t need a credit card and can start listing properties immediately.</p> </div> </div> </div> </details> <details id="e-n-accordion-item-1441" class="e-n-accordion-item"> <summary class="e-n-accordion-item-title" data-accordion-index="2" tabindex="-1" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="e-n-accordion-item-1441"> <span class='e-n-accordion-item-title-header'><p class="e-n-accordion-item-title-text"> What are the benefits of using property management software? </p></span> <span class='e-n-accordion-item-title-icon'> <span class='e-opened'><svg aria-hidden="true" class="e-font-icon-svg e-fas-caret-up" viewbox="0 0 320 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M288.662 352H31.338c-17.818 0-26.741-21.543-14.142-34.142l128.662-128.662c7.81-7.81 20.474-7.81 28.284 0l128.662 128.662c12.6 12.599 3.676 34.142-14.142 34.142z"></path></svg></span> <span class='e-closed'><svg aria-hidden="true" class="e-font-icon-svg e-fas-caret-down" viewbox="0 0 320 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M31.3 192h257.3c17.8 0 26.7 21.5 14.1 34.1L174.1 354.8c-7.8 7.8-20.5 7.8-28.3 0L17.2 226.1C4.6 213.5 13.5 192 31.3 192z"></path></svg></span> </span> </summary> <div role="region" aria-labelledby="e-n-accordion-item-1441" class="elementor-element elementor-element-b3b7bfd e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="b3b7bfd" data-element_type="container" data-settings="{&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;}"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-48e2119 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="48e2119" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <span style="font-weight: 400;">For time-strapped landlords and property managers of all stripes, the key benefit of using all-in-one software for property management solution boils down to time savings. You’ll be much more efficient at running your business because you can automate the mundane everyday tasks that eat your time.</span> <span style="font-weight: 400;">Let’s break down a few more benefits you’ll gain from property manager software.</span> <p style="font-weight: 400;color: var(--e-global-color-primary);font-family: &quot;Poppins&quot;,Sans-serif;font-size: 22px;">Tenant Management</p> <span style="font-weight: 400;">Using the best rental property management software, like TurboTenant, provides tenants with a portal from which they can submit maintenance requests, pay rent, and review their lease. It empowers tenants and helps them feel heard when issues arise.</span> <p style="font-weight: 400;color: var(--e-global-color-primary);font-family: &quot;Poppins&quot;,Sans-serif;font-size: 22px;">Financial Management</p> <span style="font-weight: 400;">A spreadsheet can be helpful; there’s no doubt about it. But, when you can link all of the financial aspects of your property management business into a single location, you won’t need to input figures manually.</span> <span style="font-weight: 400;">Instead, when rent payments flow in, they’re automatically tracked as revenue, and when you have an expense, the property management software accounts for it. It’s an easy way to improve your financial accuracy so you always know where you stand.</span> <p style="font-weight: 400;color: var(--e-global-color-primary);font-family: &quot;Poppins&quot;,Sans-serif;font-size: 22px;">Scalability</p> <span style="font-weight: 400;">As the number of properties you own grows, the administrative work to manage them does as well.</span> <span style="font-weight: 400;">Property management software reduces your workload. As your number of properties increases, the software&#8217;s automation handles all the tedious manual work that would require you to hire help or spend your long nights doing it yourself.</span> <p style="font-weight: 400;color: var(--e-global-color-primary);font-family: &quot;Poppins&quot;,Sans-serif;font-size: 22px;">Improved Tenant Satisfaction</p> <span style="font-weight: 400;">Most tenants are used to paying for things online; why should rent be any different? Providing them with the tools to pay their rent via ACH, debit, or credit card modernizes your business over checks and money orders and gives your tenants options.</span> <span style="font-weight: 400;">According to internal TurboTenant data, 66.09% of tenants pay their rent via debit card, ACH, or credit card. It’s essential to provide tenants with the tools they need to complete their most critical task: paying rent, and TurboTenant’s free property management software can help you do that.</span> </div> </div> </div> </details> <details id="e-n-accordion-item-1442" class="e-n-accordion-item"> <summary class="e-n-accordion-item-title" data-accordion-index="3" tabindex="-1" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="e-n-accordion-item-1442"> <span class='e-n-accordion-item-title-header'><p class="e-n-accordion-item-title-text"> What features should I look for in property management software? Plus, our rent collection software lets you send automatic rent reminders, apply late fees, and distribute receipts digitally. It might be the most important property management software feature of them all. <p style="font-weight: 400;color: var(--e-global-color-primary);font-family: &quot;Poppins&quot;,Sans-serif;font-size: 22px;">Accounting</p> <a href="https://www.turbotenant.com/rental-accounting/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">TurboTenant accounting</a> enables you to get rid of those spreadsheets and Quickbooks and, finally, utilize tools built specifically for property managers and landlords. With it, you can automate the most tedious aspects of running your business. Then, with just a few clicks, generate reports that make tax time less stressful. jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
    // Create a MutationObserver to watch for the .close-popup and .dialog-close-button elements
    const observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
        // Check if .close-popup and .dialog-close-button exist and are ready for binding
        const customCloseButton = $(".close-popup");
        const closeIcon = $(".dialog-close-button");

        if (customCloseButton.length && closeIcon.length) {
            // Bind the click event to .close-popup to trigger the close action on .dialog-close-button
            customCloseButton.on("click", function() {
                closeIcon.click();
            });

            // Disconnect the observer after binding to prevent multiple bindings
            observer.disconnect();
        }
    });

    // Start observing the document for added nodes in the DOM
    observer.observe(document.body, {
        childList: true,
        subtree: true
    });
});
</script> <script nitro-exclude>

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    const form = document.getElementById('custom-form');
    const message = document.getElementById('form-message');

    if (form) {
        form.addEventListener('submit', async function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();

            const formData = new FormData(form);

            try {
                const response = await fetch('/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php?action=submit_form_to_customerio', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    body: formData,
                });

                const result = await response.json();

                if (response.ok && result.success) {
                    message.textContent = 'Form submitted successfully!';
                    message.style.color = 'green';
                    form.reset();
                } else {
                    message.textContent = 'An error occurred. Please try again.';
                    message.style.color = 'red';
                    console.error(result.data || 'Error occurred');
                }
            } catch (error) {
                message.textContent = 'An error occurred. Please try again.';
                message.style.color = 'red';
                console.error('Error:', error);
            }
        });
    }
});

 document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  // Check if 'ajs_user_id' cookie exists
  var isRegisteredUser = document.cookie.split(';').some(function(item) {
   return item.trim().startsWith('ajs_user_id=');
  });

  // Set 'registered_user' cookie
  var registeredUserValue = isRegisteredUser ? 'true' : 'false';
  document.cookie = 'registered_user=' + registeredUserValue + ';path=/;max-age=' + (86400 * 30);

  // Manage 'unregistered_user_page_view_count' cookie
  if (!isRegisteredUser) {
   var count = 1;
   var existingCount = document.cookie.split(';').find(row => row.trim().startsWith('unregistered_user_page_view_count='));
   if (existingCount) {
    count = parseInt(existingCount.split('=')[1]) + 1;
   }
   document.cookie = 'unregistered_user_page_view_count=' + count + ';path=/;max-age=' + (86400 * 30);
  } else {
   var count = 0;
   document.cookie = 'unregistered_user_page_view_count=' + count + ';path=/;max-age=' + (86400 * 30);
  }
  
  // Check if this is a new browsing session
  if (!isRegisteredUser && !sessionStorage.getItem('sessionCounted')) {
   sessionStorage.setItem('sessionCounted', 'true');

   var count = 1;
   var existingCount = document.cookie.split(';').find(row => row.trim().startsWith('unregistered_user_session_count='));
   if (existingCount) {
    count = parseInt(existingCount.split('=')[1]) + 1;
   }
   document.cookie = 'unregistered_user_session_count=' + count + ';path=/;max-age=' + (86400 * 30);
  } else {
   var count = 0;
   document.cookie = 'unregistered_user_session_count=' + count + ';path=/;max-age=' + (86400 * 30);
  }
 });

         lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );

        lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );

function mixPanelEvent(mpEvent,mpLocation) {
  if (window.mixpanel) {
    window.mixpanel.track(mpEvent, {
      location: mpLocation
    });
  }
}

const mpTriggers = document.querySelectorAll(".mp-trigger");

mpTriggers.forEach((target) => {
  target.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
    //get the event name
    const mpEvent = target.getAttribute('data-mp-event');
  //get the location
  const dataLocation = target.getAttribute('data-mp-location');
  const defaultLocation = 'location not available';
  const mpLocation = dataLocation || defaultLocation;
    //fire event
    mixPanelEvent(mpEvent,mpLocation);
  });
});    
</script> <script>
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
        // Function to get UTM parameters from the URL
        function getUTMParams() {
            const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
            const utmParams = {};

            // Loop through UTM parameters and store them
            ['utm_source', 'utm_medium', 'utm_campaign', 'utm_term', 'utm_content'].forEach(param => {
                if (urlParams.has(param)) {
                    utmParams[param] = urlParams.get(param);
                    console.log(`UTM Parameter found: ${param} = ${utmParams[param]}`);
                }
            });

            console.log('All UTM Parameters:', utmParams);
            return utmParams;
        }

        // Function to add UTM parameters to each app.link
        function appendUTMParamsToAppLinks() {
            const utmParams = getUTMParams();

            if (Object.keys(utmParams).length === 0) {
                console.log('No UTM parameters found in the URL. Exiting function.');
                return; // Exit if no UTM parameters
            }

            // Select all links with "app.link" in the href
            document.querySelectorAll('a[href*="app.link"]').forEach(function(link) {
                const currentUrl = new URL(link.href);
                console.log(`Original app.link URL: ${currentUrl}`);

                // Append each UTM parameter to the link
                Object.keys(utmParams).forEach(param => {
                    currentUrl.searchParams.set(param, utmParams[param]);
                    console.log(`Adding ${param}=${utmParams[param]} to ${currentUrl}`);
                });

                // Convert the URL to a string and decode it to replace &amp; with &
                const finalUrl = decodeURIComponent(currentUrl.toString());

                link.href = finalUrl; // Update link href
                console.log(`Updated app.link URL: ${finalUrl}`);
            });
        }

        // Call the function to update links
        appendUTMParamsToAppLinks();
    });
